I've created a comprehensive **6-agent orchestrated system** for Angular migrations (19, 20, 21) with **minimal developer configuration required**.

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```
Type: @agents Migration Orchestrator
```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

### **Key Features**

✅ **Minimal Setup**
- Auto-detects workspace structure
- Auto-creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

✅ **Comprehensive**
- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)
- PrimeNG migration (v17→v19/v20/v21)
- Nx migration (if applicable)
- @onecx package updates (per documented versions)
- 50+ line error capture for all failures

✅ **Orchestrated**
- Single source of truth: MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Halt-based: Developer confirmation after each step
- Session resumption: Can pause/resume across chats
- Error systematic resolution: EVERY error fixed

✅ **Generalized**
- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21
- Adapts to Nx or standalone Angular
- Customizable via USER_CUSTOM_RULES.md

## ✅ **Agent Orchestration System Complete**

I've created a comprehensive **6-agent orchestrated system** for Angular migrations (19, 20, 21) with **minimal developer configuration required**.

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```
Type: @agents Migration Orchestrator
```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

### **Key Features**

✅ **Minimal Setup**
- Auto-detects workspace structure
- Auto-creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

✅ **Comprehensive**
- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)
- PrimeNG migration (v17→v19/v20/v21)
- Nx migration (if applicable)
- @onecx package updates (per documented versions)
- 50+ line error capture for all failures

✅ **Orchestrated**
- Single source of truth: MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Halt-based: Developer confirmation after each step
- Session resumption: Can pause/resume across chats
- Error systematic resolution: EVERY error fixed

✅ **Generalized**
- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21
- Adapts to Nx or standalone Angular
- Customizable via USER_CUSTOM_RULES.md

### **What Was Created**

### **How to Use**

- Orchestrator checks prerequisites

- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21

I've created a comprehensive **6-agent orchestrated system** for Angular migrations (19, 20, 21) with **minimal developer configuration required**.

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```

```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

- Auto-detects workspace structure

- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)

- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```

```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```
Type: @agents Migration Orchestrator
```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

### **Key Features**

✅ **Minimal Setup**
- Auto-detects workspace structure
- Auto-creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

✅ **Comprehensive**
- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)
- PrimeNG migration (v17→v19/v20/v21)
- Nx migration (if applicable)
- @onecx package updates (per documented versions)
- 50+ line error capture for all failures

✅ **Orchestrated**
- Single source of truth: MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Halt-based: Developer confirmation after each step
- Session resumption: Can pause/resume across chats
- Error systematic resolution: EVERY error fixed

✅ **Generalized**
- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21
- Adapts to Nx or standalone Angular
- Customizable via USER_CUSTOM_RULES.md

- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

## ✅ **Agent Orchestration System Complete**

I've created a comprehensive **6-agent orchestrated system** for Angular migrations (19, 20, 21) with **minimal developer configuration required**.

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```
Type: @agents Migration Orchestrator
```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

### **Key Features**

✅ **Minimal Setup**
- Auto-detects workspace structure
- Auto-creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

✅ **Comprehensive**
- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)
- PrimeNG migration (v17→v19/v20/v21)
- Nx migration (if applicable)
- @onecx package updates (per documented versions)
- 50+ line error capture for all failures

✅ **Orchestrated**
- Single source of truth: MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Halt-based: Developer confirmation after each step
- Session resumption: Can pause/resume across chats
- Error systematic resolution: EVERY error fixed

✅ **Generalized**
- Works for Angular 19, 20, 21
- Adapts to Nx or standalone Angular
- Customizable via USER_CUSTOM_RULES.md

## ✅ **Agent Orchestration System Complete**

I've created a comprehensive **6-agent orchestrated system** for Angular migrations (19, 20, 21) with **minimal developer configuration required**.

### **What Was Created** 

Located in agents and .github:

| Agent | Purpose | Role |
|-------|---------|------|
| 🎯 **Migration Orchestrator** | Master coordinator | **START HERE** - Manages phases 1→A→B→C |
| 🔍 **Phase 1 Initializer** | Documentation discovery | Finds all docs, extracts packages, creates plan |
| 🛠️ **Phase A Pre-migration** | Task execution | Runs pre-migration tasks + halts for confirmation |
| ⚡ **Phase B Core Upgrade** | Framework upgrade | Executes core Angular upgrade (or cheat sheet) |
| 🔧 **Phase C Post-migration** | Stabilization | Fixes errors, migrates PrimeNG/Nx, validates |
| ✅ **Validation Executor** | Build/Lint/Test | Runs npm commands in strict order |

### **How to Use**

**Step 1: In VS Code Chat**
```
Type: @agents Migration Orchestrator
```

**Step 2: Follow Workflow**
- Orchestrator checks prerequisites
- Phase 1 discovers docs & creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Developer reviews plan → types "start"
- Phase A executes tasks (with halts for "next" confirmations)
- Phase B handles core upgrade (Assistant executes by default)
- Phase C fixes errors & migrates frameworks
- Final validation confirms completion

### **Key Features**

✅ **Minimal Setup**
- Auto-detects workspace structure
- Auto-creates MIGRATION_PROGRESS.md
- Auto-starts MCP servers
- No manual file creation needed

✅ **Comprehensive**
- Build/Lint/Test strict order (ALWAYS enforced)
